\V[Variable ID]: Prints the value of a specific variable. Ex) \V0: Prints the value of variable 0\r\n\WV[Variable ID]: Prints the value of a specific world variable. Ex) \WV0: Prints the value of world variable 0\r\n\WSV[Variable ID] : Prints the value of a specific world String variable Ex) \WSV0 : Prints the value of world String variable "text"\r\n\G: Prints the player's gold.\r\n\$: Prints the player's gold.\r\n\C0 ~ \C9: colors the text. (0 to 9)\r\n\S0 ~ \S9: Adjusts the text print speed. (0 to 9, the lower the faster)\r\n\N: Prints the name of the user.\r\n\! : Stop printing, you must touch to start again.\r\n\ | : Wait 2 seconds.\r\n\. : Wait 0.5 seconds.\r\n\^: Close the dialog window immediately.\r\n\_: Insert a blank space.\r\n\> [Text] \ <: Prints a specific text at once.\r\n\C#FF0000 Colors the text (Hex:Red: FF0000)
